OBJECT Report 16521 Form 27EQ Correction
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=29-09-16;
    Time=12:00:00 PM;
    Version List=NAVIN9.00.00.47042;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[ENU=Form 27EQ Correction;
               ENN=Form 27EQ Correction];
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  CompanyInformation.GET;
                  IF CurrentQuarter = 0 THEN
                    ERROR(Text16500);
                  IF FinancialYear = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16501);
                  IF TCANLocation = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16502);
                  IF PersonName = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16503);
                  IF Designation = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16504);
                  IF PrintingDate = 0D THEN
                    ERROR(Text16505);
                  IF PANNo = '' THEN
                    ERROR(PANNoEmptyErr);
                  IF CompanyInformation."Phone No." = '' THEN
                    ERROR(CompInfoPhoneNoEmptyErr);
                  IF CompanyInformation."E-Mail" = '' THEN
                    ERROR(CompInfoEmailEmptyErr);
                  IF CompanyInformation."Location Code" = '' THEN
                    ERROR(CompInfoLocationEmptyErr);

                  TCSChallanRegister.RESET;
                  TCSChallanRegister.SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                  IF NOT TCSChallanRegister.FIND('-') THEN
                    ERROR(Text16506,'Financial Year');
                  TCSChallanRegister.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                  IF NOT TCSChallanRegister.FIND('-') THEN
                    ERROR(Text16506,'Quarter');
                  TCSChallanRegister.SETRANGE("T.C.A.N. No.",TCANLocation);
                  IF TCSChallanRegister.FIND('-') THEN
                    REPEAT
                      IF (TCSChallanRegister."Challan No." = '') OR ((TCSChallanRegister."BSR Code" = '') AND
                                                                     (CompanyInformation."Company Status" <>
                                                                      CompanyInformation."Company Status"::Government))
                      THEN
                        ERROR(Text16508);
                      Form27EQEntry.RESET;
                      Form27EQEntry.SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                      IF NOT Form27EQEntry.FIND('-') THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'Financial Year');
                      Form27EQEntry.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                      IF NOT Form27EQEntry.FIND('-') THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'Quarter');
                      IF NOT Form27EQEntry.FIND('-') THEN
                        ERROR(Text16507);
                      Form27EQEntry.SETRANGE("T.C.A.N. No.",TCANLocation);
                      IF NOT Form27EQEntry.FIND('-') THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'T.C.A.N No.');
                      Form27EQEntry.SETRANGE(Printed,TRUE);
                      Form27EQEntry.SETRANGE("Challan Register Entry No.",TCSChallanRegister."Entry No.");
                      Execute += Form27EQEntry.COUNT;
                    UNTIL TCSChallanRegister.NEXT = 0;

                  IF (CompanyInformation."Company Status" <> CompanyInformation."Company Status"::Government) AND
                     (STRLEN(MobileNo) <> 10)
                  THEN
                    ERROR(Text16520);
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 9977;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table16515;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Entry No.)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(No. of Revision=FILTER(<>0));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                               SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                               SETRANGE("Collector T.C.A.N. No.",TCANLocation);
                               SETRANGE(Revised,TRUE);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  "Responsible Person Name" := PersonName;
                                  MODIFY;
                                  Form27EQEntry.GET("Entry No.");
                                  Form27EQEntry.Printed := TRUE;
                                  Form27EQEntry.MODIFY;
                                  IF NOT (Filed OR Revised) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF Quarter = Quarter::Q4 THEN
                                    Year := COPYSTR(FORMAT("Assessment Year"),1,4)
                                  ELSE
                                    Year := COPYSTR(FORMAT("Financial Year"),1,4);

                                  IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q1 THEN
                                    MonthText := Text16509
                                  ELSE
                                    IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q2 THEN
                                      MonthText := Text16510
                                    ELSE
                                      IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q3 THEN
                                        MonthText := Text16511
                                      ELSE
                                        IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q4 THEN
                                          MonthText := Text16512;

                                  State.SETFILTER("State Code for eTDS/TCS","Collector State");
                                  IF State.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    StateDescription := State.Description;

                                  // IF "Collector Category" = "Collector Category"::"0" THEN
                                  // CollectorType := Text16513;
                                  // IF "Collector Category" = "Collector Category"::"1" THEN
                                  // CollectorType := Text16514;
                                  CollectorType := "Collector Category";
                                  IfFiled := Text16515;

                                  IF "Original RRR No." <> '' THEN
                                    IfFiled := Text16516;

                                  Num := 0;
                                  Num2 := 0;
                                  ChallanRegisterEntryNo := 0;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 5365;1   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table16517;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Challan Register Entry No.)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Challan Register Entry No.=FILTER(<>0),
                                       No. of Revision=FILTER(<>0));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS("Total TCS Including SHE CESS","TCS Amount",
                                 TotalTaxCollected,"eCESS Amount","Surcharge Amount",TotalValue);

                               SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                               SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                               SETRANGE(Revised,TRUE);
                               SETRANGE("T.C.A.N. No.",TCANLocation);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice THEN
                                    AdjustAppliedEntries("Form 27EQ Entry");
                                  Form27EQEntry2.GET("Entry No.");
                                  Form27EQEntry2.Printed := TRUE;
                                  Form27EQEntry2.MODIFY;
                                  IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF ChallanRegisterEntryNo <> "Challan Register Entry No." THEN BEGIN
                                    TotalTCSIncludingeCESS := 0;
                                    Form27EQEntry.SETRANGE("Challan Register Entry No.","Challan Register Entry No.");
                                    IF Form27EQEntry.FIND('-') THEN
                                      REPEAT
                                        TotalTCSIncludingeCESS += Form27EQEntry."Total TCS Including SHE CESS";
                                      UNTIL Form27EQEntry.NEXT = 0;

                                    IF CurrentQuarter > 0 THEN BEGIN
                                      IncomeTaxAccountingPeriod.SETRANGE("Financial Year for eTDS/TCS",FinancialYear);
                                      IF IncomeTaxAccountingPeriod.FINDFIRST THEN
                                        TDSTCSPeriodSetup.RESET;
                                      TDSTCSPeriodSetup.SETRANGE("No.",IncomeTaxAccountingPeriod."No.");
                                      TDSTCSPeriodSetup.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                                      IF TDSTCSPeriodSetup.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                        EndDate := COPYSTR(FORMAT(TDSTCSPeriodSetup."Ending Date"),1,6);
                                        EndDate1 := COPYSTR(FORMAT(TDSTCSPeriodSetup."Ending Date"),7,8);
                                      END;
                                    END;

                                    Num3 := 0;
                                    InvoiceAmount := 0;
                                    "TCS Challan Register".SETRANGE("Challan No.","Challan No.");
                                    IF "TCS Challan Register".FINDFIRST THEN;

                                    ChallanRegisterEntryNo := "Challan Register Entry No.";
                                  END;

                                  IF "Party Code1" = '1' THEN
                                    CollectorCode := Text16517
                                  ELSE
                                    CollectorCode := Text16518;

                                  TotalTaxCollected := ("TCS Amount" + "Surcharge Amount" + "eCESS Amount" + "SHE CESS Amount");

                                  Rate := "TCS %" + ("TCS %" * "Surcharge %" / 100);
                                  RateAtWhichCollected := Rate + (Rate * ("eCESS %" + "SHE CESS %") / 100);

                                  Num3 := Num3 + 1;
                                  InvoiceAmount += ABS("Invoice Amount");

                                  IF "Concessional Code" = '' THEN
                                    "Concessional Code" := Text16519;

                                  CertificateNo := '';
                                  IF "Concessional Code" = 'A' THEN BEGIN
                                    NodNocCertificate.RESET;
                                    NodNocCertificate.SETRANGE(Type,"Party Type");
                                    NodNocCertificate.SETRANGE("No.","Party Code");
                                    IF NodNocCertificate.FINDFIRST THEN
                                      CertificateNo := NodNocCertificate."Certificate No.";
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Quarter=FIELD(Quarter),
                            Financial Year=FIELD(Financial Year) }

                               TDSTCSPeriodSetup.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);

                                   FinancialYear := IncomeTaxAccountingPeriod."Financial Year for eTDS/TCS";
                               END;
                             END;
                           END;
                            }

    PROCEDURE AdjustAppliedEntries@1(VAR Form27EQEntry2@1500003 : Record 16517);
    VAR
      DtldCustLedgEntry1@1001 : Record 379;
      DtldCustLedgEntry2@1000 : Record 379;
      CustLedEntry@1500001 : Record 21;
      CustLedEntry2@1500002 : Record 21;
      Form27EQEntry3@1500000 : Record 16517;
    BEGIN
      CustLedEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.");
      CustLedEntry.SETRANGE("Document No.",Form27EQEntry2."Document No.");
      IF NOT CustLedEntry.FINDFIRST THEN
        EXIT;

      DtldCustLedgEntry1.SETCURRENTKEY("Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
      DtldCustLedgEntry1.SETRANGE("Cust. Ledger Entry No.",CustLedEntry."Entry No.");
      DtldCustLedgEntry1.SETRANGE(Unapplied,FALSE);
      IF DtldCustLedgEntry1.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          IF DtldCustLedgEntry1."Cust. Ledger Entry No." =
             DtldCustLedgEntry1."Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No."
          THEN BEGIN
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.INIT;
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.SETCURRENTKEY("Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No.","Entry Type");
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.SETRANGE(
              "Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No.",DtldCustLedgEntry1."Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.SETRANGE("Entry Type",DtldCustLedgEntry2."Entry Type"::Application);
            DtldCustLedgEntry2.SETRANGE(Unapplied,FALSE);
            IF DtldCustLedgEntry2.FIND('-') THEN
              REPEAT
                IF DtldCustLedgEntry2."Cust. Ledger Entry No." <>
                   DtldCustLedgEntry2."Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No."
                THEN BEGIN
                  CustLedEntry2.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
                  CustLedEntry2.SETRANGE("Entry No.",DtldCustLedgEntry2."Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
                  IF CustLedEntry2.FIND('-') THEN
                    CustLedEntry2.MARK(TRUE);
                END;
              UNTIL DtldCustLedgEntry2.NEXT = 0;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            CustLedEntry2.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry No.");
            CustLedEntry2.SETRANGE("Entry No.",DtldCustLedgEntry1."Applied Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
            IF CustLedEntry2.FIND('-') THEN
              CustLedEntry2.MARK(TRUE);
          END;
        UNTIL DtldCustLedgEntry1.NEXT = 0;

      CustLedEntry2.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);

      IF CustLedEntry2.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          Form27EQEntry3.SETRANGE("Document No.",CustLedEntry2."Document No.");
          IF Form27EQEntry3.FINDFIRST THEN
            IF Form27EQEntry3."TCS Paid" THEN
              IF Form27EQEntry3."Document Type" <> Form27EQEntry3."Document Type"::Payment THEN BEGIN
                Form27EQEntry2."Invoice Amount" += Form27EQEntry3."Invoice Amount";
                Form27EQEntry2."TCS Base Amount" += Form27EQEntry3."TCS Base Amount";
                Form27EQEntry2."Surcharge Base Amount" += Form27EQEntry3."Surcharge Base Amount";

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
